You commence the game by first placing a bet. Cards are dealt in rotation from left to right starting from the Dealer. The dealer’s hand will have one card face up and another face down. If your card totals closer to 21 and is more than the Dealer’s hand, then you win.\r\n\r\nSplit\r\n\r\nWhen your hands consists of two of the same cards, you have the option to split. The dealer is dealt two cards, and the player is dealt two cards in each box. \r\n- The player’s cards are dealt face up, while only the dealer’s first card is shown.\r\n- You can decide to Hit, Double, Split, or Stand.\r\n- Depending on your cards and the dealer’s card, you may additionally have the options to split, take even money or take insurance.\r\n- If you decide to Hit, Double, or
